## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-117">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-117">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-118">No Visual Studio, um projeto ASP.NET Core usa como padrão a hospedagem [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-118">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-119">Uma *falha de 502,5 processo* ou uma *falha de início de 500,30* que ocorre quando a depuração local pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-119">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-120">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-120">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-121">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-121">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-122">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-122">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-123">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-123">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-124">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-124">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-125">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-125">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-126">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-126">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-127">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-127">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-128">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-128">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-129">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-129">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-130">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-130">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-131">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-131">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-132">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas**do **Gerenciador do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-132">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-133">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-133">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-134">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-134">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-135">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-135">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-136">Erro interno de servidor 500</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-136">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-137">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-137">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-138">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-138">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-139">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-139">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-140">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-140">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-141">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-141">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-142">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-142">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-143">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-143">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-144">500.0 Falha de carregamento de manipulador em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-144">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-145">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-145">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-146">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-146">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-147">Erro desconhecido ao carregar ASP.NET Core componentes do [módulo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-147">An unknown error occurred loading [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-148">Execute uma das seguintes ações:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-148">Take one of the following actions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-149">Entre em contato com o [Suporte da Microsoft](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (selecione **Ferramentas para Desenvolvedores** e, em seguida, **ASP.NET Core**).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-149">Contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (select **Developer Tools** then **ASP.NET Core**).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-150">Faça uma pergunta no Stack Overflow.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-150">Ask a question on Stack Overflow.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-151">Registre um problema no nosso [Repositório do GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-151">File an issue on our [GitHub repository](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span></span>

### <a name="50030-in-process-startup-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-152">500.30 Falha de inicialização em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-152">500.30 In-Process Startup Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-153">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-153">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-154">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-154">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-155">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o .NET Core CLR em processo, mas falha ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-155">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core CLR in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-156">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-156">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-157">Condições comuns de falha:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-157">Common failure conditions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-158">O aplicativo está configurado incorretamente devido ao direcionamento de uma versão do ASP.NET Core estrutura compartilhada que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-158">The app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-159">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-159">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-160">Usando Azure Key Vault, falta de permissões para o Key Vault.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-160">Using Azure Key Vault, lack of permissions to the Key Vault.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-161">Verifique as políticas de acesso no Key Vault de destino para garantir que as permissões corretas sejam concedidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-161">Check the access policies in the targeted Key Vault to ensure that the correct permissions are granted.</span></span>

### <a name="50031-ancm-failed-to-find-native-dependencies"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-162">500.31 O ANCM não pôde encontrar dependências nativas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-162">500.31 ANCM Failed to Find Native Dependencies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-163">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-163">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-164">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-164">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-165">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o tempo de execução do .NET Core em processo, mas falha ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-165">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core runtime in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-166">A causa mais comum dessa falha de inicialização é quando o runtime `Microsoft.NETCore.App` ou `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` não está instalado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-166">The most common cause of this startup failure is when the `Microsoft.NETCore.App` or `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` runtime isn't installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-167">Se o aplicativo for implantado no ASP.NET Core 3.0 de destino e essa versão não existir no computador, esse erro ocorrerá.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-167">If the app is deployed to target ASP.NET Core 3.0 and that version doesn't exist on the machine, this error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-168">Segue um exemplo de mensagem de erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-168">An example error message follows:</span></span>

```
The specified framework 'Microsoft.NETCore.App', version '3.0.0' was not found.
  - The following frameworks were found:
      2.2.1 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview5-27626-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27713-13 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27714-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27723-08 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
```

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-169">A mensagem de erro lista todas as versões instaladas do .NET Core e a versão solicitada pelo aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-169">The error message lists all the installed .NET Core versions and the version requested by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-170">Para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-170">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-171">Instale a versão adequada do .NET Core no computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-171">Install the appropriate version of .NET Core on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-172">Altere o aplicativo para uma versão do .NET Core que está presente no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-172">Change the app to target a version of .NET Core that's present on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-173">Publique o aplicativo como uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-173">Publish the app as a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-174">Durante a execução no desenvolvimento (quando a variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` está definida como `Development`), o erro específico é gravado na resposta HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-174">When running in development (the `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` environment variable is set to `Development`), the specific error is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-175">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo também é encontrada no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-175">The cause of a process startup failure is also found in the Application Event Log.</span></span>

### <a name="50032-ancm-failed-to-load-dll"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-176">500.32 O ANCM não pôde carregar o dll</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-176">500.32 ANCM Failed to Load dll</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-177">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-177">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-178">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-178">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-179">A causa mais comum para esse erro é que o aplicativo foi publicado para uma arquitetura de processador incompatível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-179">The most common cause for this error is that the app is published for an incompatible processor architecture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-180">Esse erro ocorrerá se o processo de trabalho estiver em execução como um aplicativo de 32 bits e o aplicativo tiver sido publicado para o destino de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-180">If the worker process is running as a 32-bit app and the app was published to target 64-bit, this error occurs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-181">Para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-181">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-182">Republique o aplicativo para a mesma arquitetura de processador que o processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-182">Republish the app for the same processor architecture as the worker process.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-183">Publique o aplicativo como uma [implantação dependente da estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-183">Publish the app as a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span></span>

### <a name="50033-ancm-request-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-184">500.33 O ANCM não pôde carregar o manipulador de solicitação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-184">500.33 ANCM Request Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-185">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-185">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-186">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-186">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-187">O aplicativo não referenciou a estrutura `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-187">The app didn't reference the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-188">Somente aplicativos direcionados à `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` estrutura podem ser hospedados pelo [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-188">Only apps targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework can be hosted by the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-189">Para corrigir esse erro, confirme se o aplicativo está direcionado para a estrutura `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-189">To fix this error, confirm that the app is targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-190">Confira o `.runtimeconfig.json` para verificar a estrutura de destino do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-190">Check the `.runtimeconfig.json` to verify the framework targeted by the app.</span></span>

### <a name="50034-ancm-mixed-hosting-models-not-supported"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-191">500.34 Não há suporte para modelos de hospedagem mistos do ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-191">500.34 ANCM Mixed Hosting Models Not Supported</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-192">O processo de trabalho não pode executar um aplicativo em processo e um aplicativo fora do processo no mesmo processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-192">The worker process can't run both an in-process app and an out-of-process app in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-193">Para corrigir esse erro, execute aplicativos em pools de aplicativos do IIS separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-193">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50035-ancm-multiple-in-process-applications-in-same-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-194">500.35 Vários aplicativos do ANCM em processo no mesmo processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-194">500.35 ANCM Multiple In-Process Applications in same Process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-195">O processo de trabalho não pode executar vários aplicativos em processo no mesmo processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-195">The worker process can't run multiple in-process apps in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-196">Para corrigir esse erro, execute aplicativos em pools de aplicativos do IIS separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-196">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50036-ancm-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-197">500.36 Falha ao carregar o manipulador de fora do processo do ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-197">500.36 ANCM Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-198">O manipulador de solicitação de fora do processo *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* não está próximo do arquivo *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-198">The out-of-process request handler, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, isn't next to the *aspnetcorev2.dll* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-199">Isso indica uma instalação corrompida do [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-199">This indicates a corrupted installation of the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-200">Para corrigir esse erro, repare a instalação do [Pacote de Hospedagem do .NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (para IIS) ou do Visual Studio (para o IIS Express).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-200">To fix this error, repair the installation of the [.NET Core Hosting Bundle](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (for IIS) or Visual Studio (for IIS Express).</span></span>

### <a name="50037-ancm-failed-to-start-within-startup-time-limit"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-201">500.37 O ANCM não pôde ser iniciado dentro do limite de tempo de inicialização</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-201">500.37 ANCM Failed to Start Within Startup Time Limit</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-202">O ANCM não pôde ser iniciado dentro do limite de tempo de inicialização fornecido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-202">ANCM failed to start within the provied startup time limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-203">Por padrão, o tempo limite é de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-203">By default, the timeout is 120 seconds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-204">Esse erro pode ocorrer ao iniciar um grande número de aplicativos no mesmo computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-204">This error can occur when starting a large number of apps on the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-205">Verifique se há picos de uso de CPU/memória no servidor durante a inicialização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-205">Check for CPU/Memory usage spikes on the server during startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-206">Talvez você precise balancear o processo de inicialização de vários aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-206">You may need to stagger the startup process of multiple apps.</span></span>

### <a name="50038-ancm-application-dll-not-found"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-207">500,38 DLL do aplicativo ANCM não encontrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-207">500.38 ANCM Application DLL Not Found</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-208">ANCM falhou ao localizar a DLL do aplicativo, que deve estar ao lado do executável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-208">ANCM failed to locate the application DLL, which should be next to the executable.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-209">Esse erro ocorre ao hospedar um aplicativo empacotado como um [executável de arquivo único](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) usando o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-209">This error occurs when hosting an app packaged as a [single-file executable](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) using the in-process hosting model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-210">O modelo em processo requer que o ANCM carregue o aplicativo .NET Core no processo existente do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-210">The in-process model requires that the ANCM load the .NET Core app into the existing IIS process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-211">Esse cenário não é suportado pelo modelo de implantação de arquivo único.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-211">This scenario isn't supported by the single-file deployment model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-212">Use **uma** das seguintes abordagens no arquivo de projeto do aplicativo para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-212">Use **one** of the following approaches in the app's project file to fix this error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-213">Desabilite a publicação de arquivo único definindo a `PublishSingleFile` Propriedade MSBuild como `false` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-213">Disable single-file publishing by setting the `PublishSingleFile` MSBuild property to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-214">Alterne para o modelo de hospedagem fora do processo definindo a `AspNetCoreHostingModel` Propriedade MSBuild como `OutOfProcess` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-214">Switch to the out-of-process hosting model by setting the `AspNetCoreHostingModel` MSBuild property to `OutOfProcess`.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-215">Falha de processo 502.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-215">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-216">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-216">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-217">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-217">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-218">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-218">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-219">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-219">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-220">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-220">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-221">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-221">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-222">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-222">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-223">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-223">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-224">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-224">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-225">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-225">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-226">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-226">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-227">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-227">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-228">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-228">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-229">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-229">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-230">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-230">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-231">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-231">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-232">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-232">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-233">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-233">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-234">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-234">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-235">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-235">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-236">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-236">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-237">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-237">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-238">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-238">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-239">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-239">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-240">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-240">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-241">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-241">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-242">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-242">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-243">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-243">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-244">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-244">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-245">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-245">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-246">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-246">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-247">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-247">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-248">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-248">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-249">Selecione **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-249">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-250">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-250">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-251">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-251">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-252">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-252">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-253">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-253">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-254">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-254">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-255">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-255">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-256">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-256">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-257">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-257">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-258">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-258">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-259">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-259">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-260">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-260">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-261">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-261">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-262">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-262">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-263">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-263">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-264">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-264">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-265">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-265">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-266">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-266">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-267">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-267">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-269">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-269">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>


     ```console

     ```

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-274">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-274">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="71cfc-292">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-292">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-293">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-293">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-294">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-294">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-295">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-295">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-296">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-296">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-297">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-297">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-298">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-298">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-299">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-299">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-300">No portal do Azure, navegue até o aplicativo Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-300">In the Azure Portal, navigate to the web app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-301">Na folha **serviço de aplicativo** , insira **kudu** na caixa de pesquisa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-301">In the **App Service** blade, enter **kudu** in the search box.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-302">Selecione **ferramentas avançadas** > **ir**para.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-302">Select **Advanced Tools** > **Go**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-303">Selecione **console de depuração > cmd**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-303">Select  **Debug console > CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-304">Navegue até *site/wwwroot*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-304">Navigate to *site/wwwroot*</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-305">Selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o arquivo de *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-305">Select the pencil icon to edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-306">No `<aspNetCore />` elemento, defina `stdoutLogEnabled="true"` e selecione **salvar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-306">In the `<aspNetCore />` element, set `stdoutLogEnabled="true"` and select **Save**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="71cfc-307">Desabilite o log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída por meio da configuração `stdoutLogEnabled="false"` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-307">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete by setting `stdoutLogEnabled="false"`.</span></span>

     1. <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-320">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-320">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-321">Edite o arquivo *web.config* selecionando o botão de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-321">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-322">Adicione a seção `<handlerSettings>` conforme mostrado em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-322">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="71cfc-323">Selecione o botão **Salvar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="71cfc-323">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
